  865   
  866   
  867     assign Constant8_out1 = 1'b1;
  868   
  869   
  870   
  871     assign Constant7_out1 = 6'b101001;
  872   
  873   
  874   
  875     always @(posedge clk or posedge reset)
  876       begin : Delay4_process
  877         if (reset == 1'b1) begin
  878           Delay4_out1 <= 1'b1;
  879         end
  880         else begin
  881           if (enb) begin
  882             Delay4_out1 <= Relational_Operator_relop1;
  883           end
  884         end
  885       end
  886   
  887   
  888   
  889     assign Logical_Operator_out1 = Constant8_out1 & Delay4_out1;
  890   
  891   
  892   
  893     always @(posedge clk or posedge reset)
  894       begin : Delay3_process
  895         if (reset == 1'b1) begin
  896           Delay3_out1 <= 6'b000000;
  897         end
  898         else begin
  899           if (enb) begin
  900             Delay3_out1 <= Add_out1;
  901           end
  902         end
  903       end
  904   
  905   
  906   
  907     assign Add_1 = {5'b0, Logical_Operator_out1};
  908     assign Add_out1 = Delay3_out1 + Add_1;
  909   
  910   
  911   
  912     assign Relational_Operator_relop1 = Add_out1 <= Constant7_out1;
  913   
  914   
  915   
  916     always @(posedge clk or posedge reset)
  917       begin : Delay1_process
  918         if (reset == 1'b1) begin
  919           Delay1_out1 <= 1'b1;
  920         end
  921         else begin
  922           if (enb) begin
  923             Delay1_out1 <= Relational_Operator_relop1;
  924           end
  925         end
  926       end
  927   
  928   
  929   
  930     // Split 32 bit word into FP sign, exponent, mantissa
  931     assign aSign = nfp_in[31];
  932     assign aExponent = nfp_in[30:23];
  933     assign aMantissa = nfp_in[22:0];
  934   
  935   
  936   
  937     always @(posedge clk or posedge reset)
  938       begin : Delay_process
  939         if (reset == 1'b1) begin
  940           Delay_out1 <= 1'b0;
  941         end
  942         else begin
  943           if (enb) begin
  944             Delay_out1 <= aSign;
  945           end
  946         end
  947       end
  948   
  949   
  950   
  951     always @(posedge clk or posedge reset)
  952       begin : Delay6_process
  953         if (reset == 1'b1) begin
  954           Delay6_reg[0] <= 1'b0;
  955           Delay6_reg[1] <= 1'b0;
  956           Delay6_reg[2] <= 1'b0;
  957           Delay6_reg[3] <= 1'b0;
  958           Delay6_reg[4] <= 1'b0;
  959           Delay6_reg[5] <= 1'b0;
  960           Delay6_reg[6] <= 1'b0;
  961           Delay6_reg[7] <= 1'b0;
  962           Delay6_reg[8] <= 1'b0;
  963           Delay6_reg[9] <= 1'b0;
  964           Delay6_reg[10] <= 1'b0;
  965           Delay6_reg[11] <= 1'b0;
  966           Delay6_reg[12] <= 1'b0;
  967           Delay6_reg[13] <= 1'b0;
